directory.\n   222→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n   223→\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n   224→\tif err != nil {\n   225→\t\treturn nil, err\n   226→\t}\n   227→\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n   228→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   229→\t}\n   230→\n   231→\tvar dms []dirMeta\n   232→\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n   233→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n   234→\t\tif err != nil {\n   235→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n   238→\t}\n   239→\treturn c.plan(dms)\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n   243→\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n   244→\t\tswitch {\n   245→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n   246→\t\t\treturn -1\n   247→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n   248→\t\t\treturn 1\n   249→\t\tdefault:\n   250→\t\t\treturn 0\n   251→\t\t}\n   252→\t})\n   253→\n   254→\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n   255→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   256→\t\treturn res, nil\n   257→\t}\n   258→\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n   259→\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n   260→\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n   261→\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n   262→\n   263→\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n   264→\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n   265→\t}\n   266→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   267→\t\treturn res, nil\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n   271→\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n   272→\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n   273→\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n   274→\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n   275→\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n   276→\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n   277→\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   278→\t\t\t}\n   279→\t\t\tbreak\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n   282→\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   283→\t\t}\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\treturn nil, nil\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n   290→// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n   291→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n   292→\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n   293→\t\treturn nil\n   294→\t}\n   295→\n   296→\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n   297→\n   298→\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n   299→\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n   300→\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n   301→\t\t\tcontinue\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\n   304→\tOuter:\n   305→\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n   306→\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n   307→\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n   308→\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n   310→\t\t\t\t}\n   311→\t\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n   314→\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n   315→\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n   316→\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n   317→\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n   318→\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n   319→\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n   320→\t\t\t\treturn p\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t}\n   323→\t}\n   324→\n   325→\treturn nil\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n   329→// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n   330→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n   331→\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n   332→\t\treturn nil\n   333→\t}\n   334→\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n   335→\t\treturn nil\n   336→\t}\n   337→\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n   338→\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n   339→\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n   340→\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   341→\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n   342→\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n   343→\t\t\t}\n   344→\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n   345→\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n   346→\t\t\tbreak\n   347→\t\t}\n   348→\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   349→\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n   350→\t\t}\n   351→\t}\n   352→\treturn overlappingDirs\n   353→}\n   354→\n   355→// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n   356→//\n   357→// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n   358→// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n   359→func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n   360→\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n   361→\n   362→\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n   363→\t\tvar (\n   364→\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n   365→\t\t\tt0    int64\n   366→\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n   367→\t\t)\n   368→\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n   369→\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n   370→\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n   371→\t\t} else {\n   372→\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n   375→\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n   376→\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   377→\t\t\ti++\n   378→\t\t\tcontinue\n   379→\t\t}\n   380→\n   381→\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n   382→\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n   383→\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n   384→\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   385→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   386→\t\t\t}\n   387→\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n   388→\t\t}\n   389→\n   390→\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n   391→\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n   392→\t\t}\n   393→\t}\n   394→\n   395→\treturn splitDirs\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n   399→// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n   400→func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n   401→\tres := &BlockMeta{\n   402→\t\tULID: uid,\n   403→\t}\n   404→\n   405→\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n   406→\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n   407→\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n   408→\n   409→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n   410→\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n   411→\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n   414→\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n   415→\t\t}\n   416→\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n   417→\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n   420→\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n   421→\t\t}\n   422→\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n   423→\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n   424→\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n   425→\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n   426→\t\t})\n   427→\t}\n   428→\tres.Compaction.Level++\n   429→\n   430→\tfor s := range sources {\n   431→\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n   432→\t}\n   433→\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n   434→\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n   435→\t})\n   436→\n   437→\tres.MinTime = mint\n   438→\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n   439→\treturn res\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n   443→// provided directories.\n   444→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   445→\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→func (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   449→\tvar (\n   450→\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n   451→\t\tbs     []*Block\n   452→\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n   453→\t\tuids   []string\n   454→\t)\n   455→\tstart := time.Now()\n   456→\n   457→\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n   458→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n   459→\t\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\n   463→\t\tvar b *Block\n   464→\n   465→\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n   466→\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n   467→\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n   468→\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n   469→\t\t\t\tb = o\n   470→\t\t\t\tbreak\n 486→\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n   487→\t}\n   488→\n   489→\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   490→\n   491→\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n   492→\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n   493→\tif err == nil {\n   494→\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   495→\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   496→\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n   497→\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n   498→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   512→\t\t\t)\n   513→\t\t} else {\n   514→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   515→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n   516→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   517→\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   519→\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   520→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   521→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   522→\t\t\t)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\treturn uid, nil\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n   528→\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   529→\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   530→\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n   531→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n   532→\t\t\t}\n   533→\t\t}\n   534→\t}\n   535→\n   536→\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n   540→\tstart := time.Now()\n   541→\n   542→\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   543→\n   544→\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n   545→\t\tULID:    uid,\n   546→\t\tMinTime: mint,\n   547→\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n   548→\t}\n   549→\tmeta.Compaction.Level = 1\n   550→\tmeta.Compaction.Sources = []ulid.ULID{uid}\n   551→\n   552→\tif base != nil {\n   553→\t\tmeta.Compaction.Parents = []BlockDesc{\n   554→\t\t\t{ULID: base.ULID, MinTime: base.MinTime, MaxTime: base.MaxTime},\n   555→\t\t}\n   556→\t\tif base.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() {\n   557→\t\t\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n   558→\t\t}\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\terr := c.write(dest, meta, DefaultBlockPopulator{}, b)\n   562→\tif err != nil {\n   563→\t\treturn uid, err\n   564→\t}\n   565→\n   566→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   567→\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   568→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"write block resulted in empty block\",\n   569→\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   570→\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   571→\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   572→\t\t)\n   573→\t\treturn ulid.ULID{}, nil\n   574→\t}\n   575→\n   576→\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   577→\t\t\"msg\", \"write block\",\n   578→\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   579→\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   580→\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   581→\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   582→\t\t\"ooo\", meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder(),\n   583→\t)\n   584→\treturn uid, nil\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// instrumentedChunkWriter is used for level 1 compactions to record statistics\n   588→// about compacted chunks.\n   589→type instrumentedChunkWriter struct {\n   590→\tChunkWriter\n   591→\n   592→\tsize    prometheus.Histogram\n   593→\tsamples prometheus.Histogram\n   594→\ttrange  prometheus.Histogram\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→func (w *instrumentedChunkWriter) WriteChunks(chunks ...chunks.Meta) error {\n   598→\tfor _, c := range chunks {\n   599→\t\tw.size.Observe(float64(len(c.Chunk.Bytes())))\n   600→\t\tw.samples.Observe(float64(c.Chunk.NumSamples()))\n   601→\t\tw.trange.Observe(float64(c.MaxTime - c.MinTime))\n   602→\t}\n   603→\treturn w.ChunkWriter.WriteChunks(chunks...)\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→// write creates a new block that is the union of the provided blocks into dir.\n   607→func (c *LeveledCompactor) write(dest string, meta *BlockMeta, blockPopulator BlockPopulator, blocks ...BlockReader) (err error) {\n   608→\tdir := filepath.Join(dest, meta.ULID.String())\n   609→\ttmp := dir + tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix\n   610→\tvar closers []io.Closer\n   611→\tdefer func(t time.Time) {\n   612→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers)).Err()\n   613→\n   614→\t\t// RemoveAll returns no error when tmp doesn't exist so it is safe to always run it.\n   615→\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   616→\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"removed tmp folder after failed compaction\", \"err\", err.Error())\n   617→\t\t}\n   618→\t\tc.metrics.Ran.Inc()\n   619→\t\tc.metrics.Duration.Observe(time.Since(t).Seconds())\n   620→\t}(time.Now())\n   621→\n   622→\tif err = os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   623→\t\treturn err\n   624→\t}\n   625→\n   626→\tif err = os.MkdirAll(tmp, 0o777); err != nil {\n   627→\t\treturn err\n   628→\t}\n   629→\n   630→\t// Populate chunk and index files into temporary directory with\n   631→\t// data of all blocks.\n   632→\tvar chunkw ChunkWriter\n   633→\n   634→\tchunkw, err = chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize(chunkDir(tmp), c.maxBlockChunkSegmentSize)\n   635→\tif err != nil {\n   636→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open chunk writer: %w\", err)\n   637→\t}\n   638→\tclosers = append(closers, chunkw)\n   639→\t// Record written chunk sizes on level 1 compactions.\n   640→\tif meta.Compaction.Level == 1 {\n   641→\t\tchunkw = &instrumentedChunkWriter{\n   642→\t\t\tChunkWriter: chunkw,\n   643→\t\t\tsize:        c.metrics.ChunkSize,\n   644→\t\t\tsamples:     c.metrics.ChunkSamples,\n   645→\t\t\ttrange:      c.metrics.ChunkRange,\n   646→\t\t}\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\tindexw, err := index.NewWriterWithEncoder(c.ctx, filepath.Join(tmp, indexFilename), c.postingsEncoder)\n   650→\tif err != nil {\n   651→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open index writer: %w\", err)\n   652→\t}\n   653→\tclosers = append(closers, indexw)\n   654→\n   655→\tif err := blockPopulator.PopulateBlock(c.ctx, c.metrics, c.logger, c.chunkPool, c.mergeFunc, blocks, meta, indexw, chunkw); err != nil {\n   656→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"populate block: %w\", err)\n   657→\t}\n   658→\n   659→\tselect {\n   660→\tcase <-c.ctx.Done():\n   661→\t\treturn c.ctx.Err()\n   662→\tdefault:\n   663→\t}\n   664→\n   665→\t// We are explicitly closing them here to check for error even\n   666→\t// though these are covered under defer. This is because in Windows,\n   667→\t// you cannot delete these unless they are closed and the defer is to\n   668→\t// make sure they are closed if the function exits due to an error above.\n   669→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n   670→\tfor _, w := range closers {\n   671→\t\terrs.Add(w.Close())\n   672→\t}\n   673→\tclosers = closers[:0] // Avoid closing the writers twice in the defer.\n   674→\tif errs.Err() != nil {\n   675→\t\treturn errs.Err()\n   676→\t}\n   677→\n   678→\t// Populated block is empty, so exit early.\n   679→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   680→\t\treturn nil\n   681→\t}\n   682→\n   683→\tif _, err = writeMetaFile(c.logger, tmp, meta); err != nil {\n   684→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write merged meta: %w\", err)\n   685→\t}\n   686→\n   687→\t// Create an empty tombstones file.\n   688→\tif _, err := tombstones.WriteFile(c.logger, tmp, tombstones.NewMemTombstones()); err != nil {\n   689→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write new tombstones file: %w\", err)\n   690→\t}\n   691→\n   692→\tdf, err := fileutil.OpenDir(tmp)\n   693→\tif err != nil {\n   694→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open temporary block dir: %w\", err)\n   695→\t}\n   696→\tdefer func() {\n   697→\t\tif df != nil {\n   698→\t\t\tdf.Close()\n   699→\t\t}\n   700→\t}()\n   701→\n   702→\tif err := df.Sync(); err != nil {\n   703→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"sync temporary dir file: %w\", err)\n   704→\t}\n   705→\n   706→\t// Close temp dir before rename block dir (for windows platform).\n   707→\tif err = df.Close(); err != nil {\n   708→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"close temporary dir: %w\", err)\n   709→\t}\n   710→\tdf = nil\n   711→\n   712→\t// Block successfully written, make it visible in destination dir by moving it from tmp one.\n   713→\tif err := fileutil.Replace(tmp, dir); err != nil {\n   714→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"rename block dir: %w\", err)\n   715→\t}\n   716→\n   717→\treturn nil\n   718→}\n   719→\n   720→type BlockPopulator interface {\n   721→\tPopulateBlock(ctx context.Context, metrics *CompactorMetrics, logger log.Logger, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc, blocks []BlockReader, meta *BlockMeta, indexw IndexWriter, chunkw ChunkWriter) error\n   722→}\n   723→\n   724→type DefaultBlockPopulator struct{}\n   725→\n   726→// PopulateBlock fills the index and chunk writers with new data gathered as the union\n   727→// of the provided blocks. It returns meta information for the new block.\n   728→// It expects sorted blocks input by mint.\n   729→func (c DefaultBlockPopulator) PopulateBlock(ctx context.Context, metrics *CompactorMetrics, logger log.Logger, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc, blocks []BlockReader, meta *BlockMeta, indexw IndexWriter, chunkw ChunkWriter) (err error) {\n   730→\tif len(blocks) == 0 {\n   731→\t\treturn errors.New(\"cannot populate block from no readers\")\n   732→\t}\n   733→\n   734→\tvar (\n   735→\t\tsets        []storage.ChunkSeriesSet\n   736→\t\tsymbols tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers); cerr != nil {\n   743→\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"close: %w\", cerr))\n   744→\t\t}\n   745→\t\terr = errs.Err()\n   746→\t\tmetrics.PopulatingBlocks.Set(0)\n   747→\t}()\n   748→\tmetrics.PopulatingBlocks.Set(1)\n   749→\n   750→\tglobalMaxt := blocks[0].Meta().MaxTime\n   751→\tfor i, b := range blocks {\n   752→\t\tselect {\n   753→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   754→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   755→\t\tdefault:\n   756→\t\t}\n   757→\n   758→\t\tif !overlapping {\n   759→\t\t\tif i > 0 && b.Meta().MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   760→\t\t\t\tmetrics.OverlappingBlocks.Inc()\n   761→\t\t\t\toverlapping = true\n   762→\t\t\t\tlevel.Info(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Found overlapping blocks during compaction\", \"ulid\", meta.ULID)\n   763→\t\t\t}\n   764→\t\t\tif b.Meta().MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   765→\t\t\t\tglobalMaxt = b.Meta().MaxTime\n   766→\t\t\t}\n   767→\t\t}\n   768→\n   769→\t\tindexr, err := b.Index()\n   770→\t\tif err != nil {\n   771→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open index reader for block %+v: %w\", b.Meta(), err)\n   772→\t\t}\n   773→\t\tclosers = append(closers, indexr)\n   774→\n   775→\t\tchunkr, err := 781→\t\ttombsr, err := b.Tombstones()\n   782→\t\tif err != nil {\n   783→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open tombstone reader for block %+v: %w\", b.Meta(), err)\n   784→\t\t}\n   785→\t\tclosers = append(closers, tombsr)\n   786→\n   787→\t\tk, v := index.AllPostingsKey()\n   788→\t\tall, err := indexr.Postings(ctx, k, v)\n   789→\t\tif err != nil {\n   790→\t\t\treturn err\n   791→\t\t}\n   792→\t\tall = indexr.SortedPostings(all)\n   793→\t\t// Blocks meta is half open: [min, max), so subtract 1 to ensure we don't hold samples with exact meta.MaxTime timestamp.\n   794→\t\tsets = append(sets, NewBlockChunkSeriesSet(b.Meta().ULID, indexr, chunkr, tombsr, all, meta.MinTime, meta.MaxTime-1, false))\n   795→\t\tsyms := indexr.Symbols()\n   796→\t\tif i == 0 {\n   797→\t\t\tsymbols = syms\n   798→\t\t\tcontinue\n   799→\t\t}\n   800→\t\tsymbols = NewMergedStringIter(symbols, syms)\n   801→\t}\n   802→\n   803→\tfor symbols.Next() {\n   804→\t\tif err := indexw.AddSymbol(symbols.At()); err != nil {\n   805→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"add symbol: %w\", err)\n   806→\t\t}\n   807→\t}\n   808→\tif err := symbols.Err(); err != nil {\n   809→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"next symbol: %w\", err)\n   810→\t}\n   811→\n   812→\tvar (\n   813→\t\tref      = storage.SeriesRef(0)\n   814→\t\tchks     []chunks.Meta\n   815→\t\tchksIter chunks.Iterator\n   816→\t)\n   817→\n   818→\tset := sets[0]\n   819→\tif len(sets) > 1 {\n   820→\t\t// Merge series using specified chunk series merger.\n   821→\t\t// The default one is the compacting series merger.\n   822→\t\tset = storage.NewMergeChunkSeriesSet(sets, mergeFunc)\n   823→\t}\n   824→\n   825→\t// Iterate over all sorted chunk series.\n   826→\tfor set.Next() {\n   827→\t\tselect {\n   828→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   829→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   830→\t\tdefault:\n   831→\t\t}\n   832→\t\ts := set.At()\n   833→\t\tchksIter = s.Iterator(chksIter)\n   834→\t\tchks = chks[:0]\n   835→\t\tfor chksIter.Next() {\n   836→\t\t\t// We are not iterating in streaming way over chunk as\n   837→\t\t\t// it's more efficient to do bulk write for index and\n   838→\t\t\t// chunk file i < steps; i++ {\n\t\tranges = append(ranges, curRange)\n\t\tcurRange *= int64(stepSize)\n\t}\n\n\treturn ranges\n}\n\n// Compactor provides compaction against an underlying storage\n// of time series data.\ntype Compactor interface {\n\t// Plan returns a set of directories that can be compacted concurrently.\n\t// The directories can be overlapping.\n\t// Results returned when compactions are in progress are undefined.\n\tPlan(dir string) ([]string, error)\n\n\t// Write persists a Block into a directory.\n\t// No Block is written when resulting Block has 0 samples, and returns empty ulid.ULID{}.\n\tWrite(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error)\n\n\t// Compact runs compaction against the provided directories. *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar dms []dirMeta\n\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n\t}\n\treturn c.plan(dms)\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn -1\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn 1\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn 0\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n\n\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n\t}\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\n// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n\n\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\tOuter:\n\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn p\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn overlappingDirs\n}\n\n// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n//\n// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\nfunc splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n\t\t\tt0    int64\n\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n\t\t)\n\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn splitDirs\n}\n\n// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\nfunc CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n\tres := &BlockMeta{\n\t\tULID: uid,\n\t}\n\n\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n\n\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n\t\t}\n\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tres.Compaction.Level++\n\n\tfor s := range sources {\n\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n\t}\n\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n\t})\n\n\tres.MinTime = mint\n\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n\treturn res\n}\n\n// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n// provided directories.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n\t\tbs     []*Block\n\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n\t\tuids   []string\n\t)\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn uid, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar b *Block\n\n\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n\t\t\t\tb = o\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif b == nil {\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tb, err = OpenBlock(c.logger, d, c.chunkPool)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn uid, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefer b.Close()\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetas = append(metas, meta)\n\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n\t\tbs = append(bs, b)\n\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n\t}\n\n\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n\n\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", b.meta.ULID,\n\t\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tb.numBytesMeta = n\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tuid = ulid.ULID{}\n\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\",\n\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn uid, nil\n\t}\n\n\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n\n\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n\t\tULID:    uid,\n\t\tMinTime: mint,\n\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n\t}\n\tmeta.Compaction.Level = {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01LM4rVs1jvoJw2rEuTMvbVj","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01CAK8mS346oN7MSFG8hJ9N1","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Operational Runbook: Prometheus TSDB Compaction\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### Purpose of Compaction\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a critical maintenance process in Prometheus that:\n\n- **Merges overlapping time blocks** into consolidated blocks that reduce query overhead and improve read performance\n- **Removes tombstoned (deleted) series** from blocks to reclaim disk space previously marked for deletion\n- **Optimizes chunk layout** to improve query performance and reduce disk I/O\n- **Manages block levels** using an exponential block range structure to balance read/write amplification\n\n### Why Compaction is Needed\n\nWithout compaction, Prometheus would accumulate:\n1. Multiple overlapping time blocks with duplicate series data → increased query time\n2. Tombstones (deletion markers) for removed series → wasted disk space\n3. Small, numerous blocks → excessive file descriptor usage and memory overhead\n\n### Block Structure and Levels\n\nPrometheus uses **leveled compaction** with exponential block ranges:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head blocks)**: Recently ingested data, 2 hours by default (controlled by `--storage.tsdb.min-block-duration`)\n- **Level 1**: 2-3 Level 0 blocks merged together\n- **Level 2**: 2-3 Level 1 blocks merged together\n- **Level N**: Progressive doubling of time ranges (2h → 10h → 50h → 250h → ...)\n\nEach level increases compaction level in block metadata:\n```\nmeta.Compaction.Level = N   # Higher = more compact\nmeta.Compaction.Parents = [list of source blocks]\nmeta.Compaction.Sources = [list of original series sources]\n```\n\n### Compaction Triggers\n\nCompaction is triggered automatically by three mechanisms:\n\n#### 1. **Time-Based Trigger (Head Compaction)**\n- Occurs when head block spans > 1.5x its configured duration\n- Formula: `MaxTime - MinTime > ChunkRange / 2 * 3`\n- Default: ~3 hours of head data → triggers compaction of ~2 hours\n- Happens continuously as new samples arrive\n\n#### 2. **Block-Level Compaction**\n- Triggered when non-overlapping blocks fall into a compactable range\n- Merges all blocks in a time range that span >= `MaxBlockDuration` (default: 2h)\n- Example: blocks covering [0-2h, 2-4h, 4-6h] merge when the range becomes [0-10h]\n\n#### 3. **Tombstone Cleanup**\n- Single blocks with > 5% of series deleted trigger standalone compaction\n- Removes tombstones and reclaims disk space\n- Helps maintain query efficiency for frequently-deleted series\n\n#### 4. **Overlapping Block Compaction (Vertical Compaction)**\n- Blocks with overlapping time ranges are merged vertically\n- Combines series from blocks that have the same timestamp range\n- Metric: `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` tracks these operations\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Activity Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | Increasing steadily, 1-5 per minute |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compaction attempts triggered | Should match or exceed `_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions | Should be 0 or very rare (<1/hour) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped (auto-compact disabled) | 0 unless feature disabled |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | Increases with out-of-order data |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time spent in compaction | p99 < 60s, p50 < 5s |\n\n#### Block Population Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Currently writing block (0 or 1) | 0 most of the time, briefly 1 during write |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Active blocks in memory | 50-200 blocks typical |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total block data on disk | < retention setting |\n\n#### Retention and Cleanup Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to cleanup tombstones | p99 < 10s |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max storage size | Set to your limit |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by time retention | 1-2 per day typical |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by size limit | Increases if space limited |\n\n#### Chunk Quality Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning | Healthy Range |\n|--------|------|---------|----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes | p99 < 32KB |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk | p99 < 500 |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range per chunk | p99 < 1000s |\n\n### Alert Thresholds\n\n#### **CRITICAL: Compaction Stuck**\n```promql\nincrease(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\nOR\n(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total - prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total) > 10\n```\n**Indicates**: Compaction is failing repeatedly or backed up\n\n#### **WARNING: High Compaction Duration**\n```promql\nhistogram_quantile(0.99, rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 60\n```\n**Indicates**: Compactions taking > 1 minute (slower than expected)\n\n#### **WARNING: Blocks Not Being Deleted**\n```promql\nincrease(prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded[1h]) == 0\nAND prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 300\n```\n**Indicates**: Blocks accumulating without compaction or deletion\n\n#### **CRITICAL: Storage Approaching Limit**\n```promql\nprometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes > 0.9\n```\n**Indicates**: Less than 10% free space in configured limit\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increases steadily (≥1 per minute during data ingestion)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is flat or very slowly increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p99 < 60 seconds\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` slowly increases then decreases (churn)\n\n**Stuck/Degraded Compaction:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` > `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` (backlog building)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increasing rapidly\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` increasing across all percentiles\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 for > 5 minutes\n- Prometheus logs show repeated \"compaction failed\" errors with consistent error message\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### Symptom\n- Compaction fails with \"no space left on device\" error\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- New samples may be rejected with \"out of disk space\" errors\n- Prometheus logs show: `msg=\"compaction failed\" err=\"mkdir ... no space\"`\n\n#### Cause\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Retention settings too high relative to available disk space\n2. Compaction temporarily requires 1.5x current data size (creates tmp block during merge)\n3. WAL (Write-Ahead Log) consuming excessive space\n4. Tombstones not being cleaned up efficiently\n5. High cardinality metrics creating more series than expected\n\n**Why it Happens:**\n- Compaction creates blocks in `.tmp-for-creation` directory while merging\n- If source blocks total 100GB and you only have 120GB free, compaction fails\n- Formula: `RequiredSpace = (CurrentBlockSize * 1.5) + WALSize`\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n```bash\n# 1. Check available disk space\ndf -h /path/to/prometheus/storage\n\n# 2. Check TSDB directory size breakdown\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/wal/\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/wbl/ 2>/dev/null  # Out-of-order WAL\n\n# 3. List blocks and their sizes\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 4. Check Prometheus logs for compaction errors\ngrep \"compaction failed\" /path/to/prometheus.log | tail -20\n\n# 5. Verify retention settings from config\ngrep -A5 \"storage:\" /path/to/prometheus.yml\n```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Increase Disk Space (Preferred)**\n1. Add more storage to the Prometheus node\n2. Monitor: `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` should remain flat\n3. Compaction should resume within 5 minutes\n\n**Option B: Reduce Retention**\n1. Stop Prometheus: `systemctl stop prometheus`\n2. Reduce retention in `prometheus.yml`:\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       cluster: prod\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention: 7d  # Reduce from current setting\n   ```\n3. Restart Prometheus: `systemctl start prometheus`\n4. Old blocks outside new retention window delete automatically during compaction\n5. Monitor: `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` should increment\n\n**Option C: Force Delete Old Blocks (Last Resort)**\n1. Identify blocks older than 30 days:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data | grep -v \"^BLOCK\" | awk '{print $1, $2}' | while read block mintime; do\n     mintime_sec=$((mintime / 1000))\n     if [ $(($(date +%s) - mintime_sec)) -gt 2592000 ]; then\n       echo \"Old block: $block ($(date -d @$mintime_sec))\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n2. **Backup first**: `tar czf prometheus_blocks_backup.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/data/`\n3. Manually delete old blocks:\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV  # OLD BLOCK ULID\n   ```\n4. Restart Prometheus to reload blocks\n5. Verify: `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` should decrease\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n#### Symptom\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` increases but `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` stays flat\n- Logs show: `msg=\"compaction failed\" err=\"...context canceled...\"` or repeated same error\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` stuck at high value\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 5 minutes\n- Queries become progressively slower as blocks accumulate\n\n#### Cause\n**Common Causes:**\n1. **Out-of-Memory (OOM)** during compaction: Large block merges require reading all chunks into memory\n2. **File Descriptor Exhaustion**: Too many open files preventing block creation\n3. **Slow Disk I/O**: Block writes timeout due to NVMe stalls or I/O contention\n4. **Lock Contention**: Compaction mutex held by other operations (deletion, reloading)\n5. **Context Cancellation**: Shutdown signal interrupting in-progress compaction\n6. **Index or Chunk Corruption**: Cannot read source block for merging\n\n**Why it Happens:**\n- Merging 3+ blocks each with millions of series requires buffering all data\n- Code reference: `tsdb/compact.go:655-729` (PopulateBlock function allocates memory for all chunks)\n- Blocks are compacted from smallest to largest, so large merged blocks consume most memory\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n```bash\n# 1. Check Prometheus memory usage\nps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n\n# 2. Check if running out of file descriptors\ncat /proc/$(pidof prometheus)/limits | grep \"open files\"\n\n# 3. Get count of open file descriptors\nlsof -p $(pidof prometheus) 2>/dev/null | wc -l\n\n# 4. Check system logs for OOM kills\ndmesg | grep -i \"killed process\" | tail -5\n\n# 5. Review Prometheus debug logs with more detail\n# Restart with log level set to debug\n# Then check logs for compaction-related messages\ngrep \"compact\\|populate\" /path/to/prometheus.log | tail -50\n\n# 6. Check if specific block is problematic\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data 01ARZ3NDEK...ULID...\n```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Step 1: Stop Compaction Temporarily**\n```bash\n# Send SIGTERM to allow graceful shutdown of current compaction\nkill -TERM $(pidof prometheus)\n\n# Wait up to 30 seconds\nsleep 30\n\n# Force kill if still running\nkill -9 $(pidof prometheus)\n```\n\n**Step 2: Identify Problem Block**\n```bash\n# Check last compaction error in logs\ntail -200 /path/to/prometheus.log | grep \"compaction failed\"\n\n# Extract block ULID from error if mentioned\n# Example: \"sources=[01ARZ3NDEK... 01ARZ3NDEM...]\"\n\n# Try to analyze the block\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data 01ARZ3NDEK...\n```\n\n**Step 3: Recover from Corruption**\nIf block is corrupted:\n```bash\n# Backup corrupted block\nmv /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK.corrupted\n\n# Restart Prometheus - it will skip corrupted block during reload\nsystemctl start prometheus\n```\n\n**Step 4: Reduce Compaction Load**\n```bash\n# Edit prometheus.yml to reduce block sizes\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    min-block-duration: 1h      # Reduce from 2h (smaller merges)\n    max-block-duration: 1h      # Prevent large blocks\n\n# OR adjust for OOM by increasing memory limits:\n#\n# In systemd service file (/etc/systemd/system/prometheus.service):\n# [Service]\n# Environment=\"GOPROC=4\"  # Limit Go processes for lower memory\n```\n\n**Step 5: Resume Prometheus**\n```bash\nsystemctl daemon-reload\nsystemctl start prometheus\n\n# Monitor recovery\nwatch -n 2 'curl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | jq \".data.result[0].value\"'\n```\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### Symptom\n- Prometheus startup fails with: `msg=\"error loading blocks\" err=\"index corrupted\"`\n- Specific block prevents database from opening\n- Query results missing data from time range of corrupted block\n- Logs show: `corrupted block <ULID>: index file corrupted` or chunk read errors\n- Cannot start Prometheus at all vs. during compaction\n\n#### Cause\n**Common Causes:**\n1. **Incomplete Block Write**: Process killed during compaction write phase\n2. **Hardware Failure**: Bit rot in block files or filesystem corruption\n3. **Incorrect Manual Edits**: Someone directly modified block files\n4. **Filesystem Corruption**: Filesystem fsck needed\n5. **WAL Replay Failure**: Head block replay produced invalid data\n6. **Failed Compaction with Failed Flag**: Block marked with `Compaction.Failed=true`\n\n**Why it Happens:**\n- Compaction creates blocks atomically (writes to .tmp-for-creation, then renames)\n- But if process dies during the close/rename, block directory left inconsistent\n- Code reference: `tsdb/db.go:574-594` (openBlocks detects corrupted blocks on startup)\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n```bash\n# 1. Check if Prometheus will start\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/path/to/prometheus/data 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# 2. Identify corrupted block from error message\n# Look for: \"corrupted block 01ARZ3NDEK...\"\n\n# 3. List all blocks and check for .tmp files\nls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/ | grep \"01ARZ3N\"\n\n# 4. Check block metadata files\ncd /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK && ls -la\n\n# 5. Try to read block with promtool\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 6. Inspect block structure\ncd /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK\nfile index chunks tombstones meta.json\n```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Option A: Remove Corrupted Block (Fastest)**\n1. Stop Prometheus\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. Backup corrupted block (for forensics)\n   ```bash\n   mv /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK /backup/01ARZ3NDEK.corrupted\n   ```\n\n3. Remove temporary directories from failed compactions\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-creation\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-deletion\" -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n4. Restart Prometheus\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Monitor startup logs\n   journalctl -u prometheus -f\n   ```\n\n5. Verify recovery\n   ```bash\n   # Check if database is now accessible\n   curl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=up | jq \".status\"\n\n   # Monitor for compaction recovery\n   curl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded | jq \".data.result[0].value\"\n   ```\n\n**Option B: Repair WAL if Head is Corrupted**\nIf the issue is with the `wal/` or `wbl/` directories:\n```bash\n# Stop Prometheus\nsystemctl stop prometheus\n\n# Backup WAL\nmv /path/to/prometheus/data/wal /backup/wal.corrupted\nmv /path/to/prometheus/data/wbl /backup/wbl.corrupted 2>/dev/null\n\n# Prometheus will replay from empty WAL on next start\nsystemctl start prometheus\n\n# Data since last block write will be lost but database will be functional\n```\n\n**Option C: Full TSDB Repair (Last Resort)**\nIf multiple blocks are corrupted:\n```bash\n# Run repair utility (if available)\ncd /path/to/prometheus\npromtool tsdb repair /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# Or manually rebuild from backup\nsystemctl stop prometheus\nrm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/*\nrestore_backup_here\nsystemctl start prometheus\n```\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n#### Symptom\n- Prometheus process killed by OOM killer: `Killed` in `ps` output\n- Logs show: `unable to allocate memory` or `malloc: out of memory`\n- `dmesg` shows: `[timestamp] Killed process 12345 (prometheus) total-vm:..., rss:..., file-cache:...`\n- Compaction consistently fails with OOM at specific block size\n- System becomes unresponsive (thrashing) before crash\n\n#### Cause\n**Root Causes:**\n1. **Large Block Merges**: Merging 3+ large blocks (each 5GB+) into memory\n2. **High Cardinality**: Millions of unique series require buffering all label combinations\n3. **Insufficient Memory**: Container/VM memory limit too low for workload\n4. **Memory Leak**: Chunk pool not releasing memory properly (Go runtime issue)\n5. **Multiple Compactions**: Several compactions running simultaneously\n\n**Why it Happens:**\n- Compaction merges multiple blocks sequentially by loading all series into memory\n- Code reference: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` (PopulateBlock loads all chunks into `[]chunks.Meta`)\n- For each series: allocates memory for all chunks across merge window\n- Formula: `MemoryNeeded ≈ NumSeries * AvgChunksPerSeries * AvgChunkSize`\n- Example: 50M series × 100 chunks × 1KB = 5GB minimum\n\n#### Diagnostic Steps\n```bash\n# 1. Check system memory usage during compaction\nwatch -n 1 'free -h && echo \"---\" && ps aux | grep prometheus'\n\n# 2. Check Prometheus memory limits\nsystemctl show prometheus --property MemoryLimit\n\n# 3. Check dmesg for OOM killer messages\ndmesg | grep \"Killed process\" | tail -5\n\n# 4. Estimate cardinality and block size\ncurl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_metric_chunks_created_total | jq \".data.result[0].value\"\n\n# 5. Check which block is causing OOM\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data | tail -5\n\n# 6. Estimate memory needed for compaction\n# Get total samples in largest 3 blocks\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data | tail -3 | awk '{s+=$5} END {print \"Total samples:\", s}'\n```\n\n#### Recovery Procedure\n\n**Step 1: Increase Memory Allocation**\n```bash\n# For systemd service:\n# Edit /etc/systemd/system/prometheus.service\n[Service]\nMemoryLimit=64G  # Increase from current value\nMemoryAccounting=yes\n\nsystemctl daemon-reload\nsystemctl restart prometheus\n```\n\n**Step 2: Reduce Block Compaction Size**\n```bash\n# Edit prometheus.yml to prevent large block merges\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    min-block-duration: 30m     # Smaller blocks = less memory per merge\n    max-block-duration: 1h      # Prevent large blocks from accumulating\n\n# Or via command-line flags\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=30m \\\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=1h\n```\n\n**Step 3: Manually Compact Blocks (Offline)**\nIf you want to reduce block sizes before restart:\n```bash\nsystemctl stop prometheus\n\n# Use promtool to compact selected blocks to smaller size\n# This creates a new block with smaller max-block-duration\npromtool tsdb create-blocks-from /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# OR manually delete newer large blocks to restart from smaller base\nls -lrht /path/to/prometheus/data/ | tail -5\n# rm /path/to/prometheus/data/01ARZ3NDEK...  # Newest block\n\nsystemctl start prometheus\n```\n\n**Step 4: Monitor Memory During Compaction**\n```bash\n# Get memory limits from Prometheus metrics\ncurl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query='process_resident_memory_bytes' | jq '.data.result[0].value'\n\n# Set up alert for approaching limit\n# HIGH_MEMORY: process_resident_memory_bytes > MemoryLimit * 0.8\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures by Scenario\n\n### Quick Reference: Compaction Failure\n\n| Error Message | Cause | Recovery |\n|---|---|---|\n| `no space left on device` | Disk full | Add storage or reduce retention |\n| `context canceled` | Shutdown during compaction | Restart Prometheus |\n| `index corrupted` | Block corruption | Remove corrupted block |\n| `cannot allocate memory` | OOM during merge | Increase memory or reduce block size |\n| `too many open files` | FD limit | Increase ulimit or reduce blocks |\n\n### Complete Recovery Checklist\n\n**For Any Compaction Failure:**\n\n1. **Isolate the Problem** (2 minutes)\n   ```bash\n   # Stop further damage\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n\n   # Check logs\n   tail -100 /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n\n   # Identify error type from above table\n   ```\n\n2. **Assess Data Impact** (5 minutes)\n   ```bash\n   # Backup TSDB directory\n   tar czf /backup/prometheus_data_$(date +%s).tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/data/\n\n   # List blocks and retention\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n3. **Apply Targeted Recovery** (5-30 minutes)\n   - Use appropriate recovery from failure modes above\n   - For unknown issues: Remove most recent block and restart\n\n4. **Verify Recovery** (5 minutes)\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Wait for startup\n   sleep 30\n\n   # Test queries\n   curl -s localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n\n   # Check for new errors\n   journalctl -u prometheus -f | grep -i error\n   ```\n\n5. **Investigate Root Cause** (10+ minutes)\n   - Check disk space trends\n   - Review memory usage patterns\n   - Verify cardinality growth\n   - Check for unexpected shutdown signals\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code Reference\n\n### Key Functions and Their Roles\n\n**Compaction Entry Points:**\n- `tsdb/db.go:1133` - `DB.Compact()` - Main compaction orchestrator, manages head and block compactions\n- `tsdb/db.go:1008-1022` - Compaction loop - Receives compaction triggers, handles failures\n\n**Compaction Planning:**\n- `tsdb/compact.go:222` - `LeveledCompactor.Plan()` - Determines which blocks can be compacted\n- `tsdb/compact.go:254` - `selectOverlappingDirs()` - Finds overlapping blocks for vertical compaction\n- `tsdb/compact.go:291` - `selectDirs()` - Finds non-overlapping blocks ready for leveled compaction\n- `tsdb/compact.go:270-284` - Tombstone-based selection - Compacts blocks with >5% deletions\n\n**Compaction Execution:**\n- `tsdb/compact.go:444` - `LeveledCompactor.Compact()` - Merges selected blocks\n- `tsdb/compact.go:607` - `LeveledCompactor.write()` - Writes new block to disk (handles tmp dirs)\n- `tsdb/compact.go:729` - `PopulateBlock()` - **Memory-intensive**: Reads all chunks and reindexes\n\n**Head Block Compaction:**\n- `tsdb/head.go:1662` - `Head.compactable()` - Checks if head span > 1.5x block duration\n- `tsdb/db.go:1166` - `rangeForTimestamp()` - Calculates compaction range for head\n- `tsdb/db.go:1162-1188` - Head compaction loop - Persists head blocks as permanent blocks\n\n**Block Loading/Deletion:**\n- `tsdb/db.go:1440` - `reloadBlocks()` - Detects and loads new compacted blocks, deletes old ones\n- `tsdb/db.go:1532` - `openBlocks()` - **Detects corrupted blocks**, marks for deletion\n- `tsdb/db.go:1606-1620` - Time retention - Deletes blocks older than retention window\n- `tsdb/db.go:1629-1645` - Size retention - Deletes blocks when total size > limit\n\n**Metrics Tracking:**\n- `tsdb/compact.go:99-151` - `NewCompactorMetrics()` - Defines all compaction metrics\n- `tsdb/db.go:261-363` - `newDBMetrics()` - Defines block/retention metrics\n- Observe: `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` in `write()` defer\n- Increment: `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` in compaction loop\n\n**Failure Handling:**\n- `tsdb/db.go:1134-1142` - Defer increments `compactionsFailed` on error return\n- `tsdb/compact.go:527-536` - Sets `Compaction.Failed` flag on source blocks if error\n- `tsdb/compact.go:494-506` - Marks source blocks deletable if output has 0 samples\n- `tsdb/db.go:574-594` - Logs corrupted blocks at startup\n\n### Metrics Implementation Details\n\n**prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds:**\n- Observed in: `tsdb/compact.go:619` - Total time including I/O and memory ops\n- Includes: Index/chunk reading, series merging, block writing, file sync\n- Measured with: `prometheus.Histogram` with 14 buckets (1s to 8192s)\n\n**prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded:**\n- Computed from: Current length of `DB.blocks` slice\n- Updated in: `reloadBlocks()` after compaction completes\n- Reflects: Active blocks available for queries\n\n---\n\n## 6. Preventive Measures\n\n### Best Practices to Avoid Compaction Issues\n\n1. **Capacity Planning**\n   ```bash\n   # Ensure disk space >= 2x average daily ingestion\n   # Compaction temporarily requires 1.5x largest block size\n   DiskNeeded = (DailyIngestionRate * RetentionDays) * 1.5\n   ```\n\n2. **Memory Sizing**\n   ```bash\n   # Rule of thumb: Memory >= (5 * UniqueMetricsCount) MB\n   # Example: 10M unique series × 5MB/M = 50GB\n   # Set: Kubernetes memory limit = 60GB for headroom\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor Key Metrics**\n   ```yaml\n   # Add to prometheus.yml\n   global:\n     scrape_interval: 30s\n\n   rule_files:\n     - 'tsdb_alerts.yml'  # Include alerts from this runbook\n   ```\n\n4. **Regular Backups**\n   ```bash\n   # Before major changes or upgrades\n   tar czf prometheus_blocks_$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/data/\n   # Store off-system\n   ```\n\n5. **Upgrade Planning**\n   - Test config changes on dev environment first\n   - Monitor first 24 hours after upgrade\n   - Have rollback plan (keep previous binary)\n\n---\n\n## 7. Emergency Contacts & Escalation\n\n**For Blocked Queries Due to Compaction:**\n1. Check if compaction is stuck using metrics above\n2. If stuck > 30 min: Stop Prometheus, remove last 2 blocks, restart\n3. Escalate to storage team if recurring\n\n**For Data Loss Concerns:**\n1. Blocks are immutable once written (safe to inspect/backup)\n2. Compaction only deletes blocks outside retention\n3. WAL is replayed on startup (recent data safe)\n\n---\n\n## Appendix A: Sample Prometheus Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\n# File: tsdb_alerts.yml\n\ngroups:\n  - name: prometheus_tsdb\n    interval: 30s\n    rules:\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionFailing\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction failing\"\n          description: \"Compaction failed {{ $value }} times in last 5 minutes\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionStuck\n        expr: |\n          (prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total - prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total) > 10\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction backlog growing\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} compactions backed up\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusOutOfDiskSpace\n        expr: |\n          (node_filesystem_avail_bytes{mountpoint=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"} /\n           node_filesystem_size_bytes{mountpoint=\"/var/lib/prometheus\"}) < 0.1\n        for: 2m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus disk space low\"\n          description: \"Less than 10% disk space available\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusHighCompactionDuration\n        expr: |\n          histogram_quantile(0.99, rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 60\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Compaction taking longer than expected\"\n          description: \"p99 compaction duration > 60 seconds\"\n\n      - alert: PrometheusBlocksAccumulating\n        expr: |\n          rate(prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded[1h]) > 0 and\n          prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 300\n        for: 1h\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus blocks accumulating\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} blocks loaded, compaction may be stuck\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Appendix B: Helpful Commands Reference\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with sizes\npromtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# Analyze specific block for issues\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data 01ARZ3NDEK...ULID\n\n# Export time series from block (debug)\npromtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data 2023-01-01T00:00:00Z 2023-01-02T00:00:00Z\n\n# Rebuild TSDB from WAL (dangerous!)\npromtool tsdb create-blocks-from wal /path/to/prometheus/data/wal /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# Check cardinality\ncurl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/label/__name__/values' | jq '. | length'\n\n# Monitor compaction in real-time\nwatch -n 5 'curl -s \"http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query_range?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total&start=$(date -d \"1 hour ago\" +%s)&end=$(date +%s)&step=60\" | jq \".data.result[0].values[-1]\"'\n\n# Check Prometheus startup for block loading errors\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/path/to/prometheus/data --log.level=debug 2>&1 | grep -i \"block\\|corrupt\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nPrometheus TSDB compaction is automated but requires operational awareness:\n\n- **Monitor** the 3 compaction success metrics and 2 resource metrics\n- **Alert** on compaction failures, backlog buildup, and resource exhaustion\n- **Recover** by identifying failure type and applying targeted fix\n- **Prevent** through proper capacity planning and regular monitoring\n\nMost compaction issues are self-healing (restarts, space, memory) but knowing the failure modes enables rapid mitigation without data loss.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":449,"cache_read_input_tokens":58755,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":449},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"18e2dfba-f00e-4332-a41f-3105ed31750a","uuid":"26eb6615-a4a3-495d-bacb-1f3ca052f7dd"}
